***geest.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>geest</a> (830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gêest</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gēst</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:geist.html>geist</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gaistaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰeysd-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵʰisd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anger, agitation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:geist.html>Geist</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">geast</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ghost</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:gast.html>gast</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>geest</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geesten.html>geesten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geestje.html>geestje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ghost, spirit</li>
<li>mind, mental conscience</li>
<li>life force, vital energy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">alchemy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> spirit, gas, distillate, essence</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>geest</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gēst</i>, a nominalization of an adjective that meant “dry, infertile”, a derivation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gais-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">infertile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">gaast</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">geast</i> (as in the Dutch/Frisian place name <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Gaasterland_(streek)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:nl:Gaasterland (streek)">Gaasterland</a></i>) and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>Geest</a></i> (which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from Low German). Other derivations of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gais-</i> are: <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gæsne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">infertility, poverty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:gast.html>gast</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">waste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">gisinn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>geest</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ghost, spirit; mind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rijk.html>rijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rich; full of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">fortuné</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fortunate, favored by fate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fortūnātus</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gefortuneerd.html>gefortuneerd</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gefortuneerd.html>gefortuneerder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">gefortuneerdst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fortunate, favored by fate</li>

***gehalte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gehalte.html>gehalte</a> (21634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gehalt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehalte.html>gehalte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehalte.html>gehalten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehaltes.html>gehaltes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gehalte.html>gehaltetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>content (numerical, as a fraction of a whole)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> CO<sub>2</sub><a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gehalte.html>gehalte</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloed.html>bloed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daalt.html>daalt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:spreken.html>spreken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> hypocapnie.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/HyperventilatieHyperventilatie_bij_de_gezonde_mens">[1]</a></sup>  |  If the CO<sub>2</sub> content in the blood falls, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> speak of hypocapnia.</dd></dl></li>
<li>value, purity (if <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> fractional content (of a valuable metal in an alloy) equals <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> purity, less impurity; thus, <a href = vnd.unilang:higher.html>higher</a> value (of the alloy as a whole, per unit of weight))
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:goud.html>Goud</a><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gehalte.html>gehalte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:karaat.html>karaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgedrukt.html>uitgedrukt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:waarbij.html>waarbij</a> 24 <a href = vnd.unilang:karaat.html>karaat</a> 100% <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gehalte_%28numismatiek%29">[2]</a></sup>  |  The purity of gold <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> expressed in carat, where 24 carat <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> 100%.</dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gehuegen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gihuggen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gahugjaną</i>.
